 chandrakant prasad singh ke blogarhu & mese saabhaar) The Reserve Bank of India has taken a big action after the Punjab National Bank scam of over Rs 12400 crore
 arabiai ne bainkon ko letters of intent jari karne kii suvidha ko khatm kar diya he
 Along with this, the Central Bank has also abolished the Letter of Comfort (loc)
 in donon instrument kaa istemaal bank apane graahakon ko guarantee dete the
 The biggest impact will be on traders who import diamond and jewelery in a big way
 visheshgyon kaa kahana he ki bhale hi lou or loc kii credit dene main bhagidaari bahut kam he
 Businessmen will not have to suffer much loss due to this, but it will definitely affect their business
 pienbi ghotaale ke baad kaarobaariyon ke liye guarantee lene kii raah kaaphi mushkil ho gaya he
 At this time, the ban on lou can be difficult
 kendriya bainkki taraf se yah karrwai punjab neshnal bank ghotaale ke baad kii gai he
 Through this decision, RBI is trying to remove the loopholes in the banking system
 lou or loc kii vyavastha khatm kiye jane ke baad kaarobaariyon ko bank letters of credit or guarantee dete rah sakate hai
 This system will continue to run smoothly
 yah vyavasthentararashtriya maanakonke mutabik he
 This arrangement strengthens the credit issuer
 darasal jab bhi ek bank kisi kaarobaari ko paise dene ke liye guarantee or locs jari karte hai, to is vyavastha ke tahat risiving bank bhi apane str par jaanch karata he
 In this system, the bank that receives the guarantee sees at its level how strong and weak the credit history of the person it is going to pay
 isse loc jari karne vaale bank kii jimmedaari kaaphi kam ho jaati he
 At the same time, speaking of lou and letter of comfort, the banks lending in it give money only on the basis of the guarantee of the issuing bank
 isamen vah apane str par kisi bhi tarah kii jaanch nahin karte hai
 Because in lou, the bank issuing it in a way guarantees that it will make the payment if the customer defaults
 bankeron kaa kahana he qilator of creditzyada surakshit hota he
 Because it also contains information of the importer, date of issue, expiry date and the goods for which it is being taken to buy
 lekin lou ke maamle main aisa nahin hota he
 Because of this, it becomes very difficult to detect disturbances in them
 lou kya he?letters of anderteking (lou) ek tarah se bank guarantee hoti he
 It is issued to make overseas payments for imports
 lou jari karne vaala bank guaranter ban jaataa he or vah apane client ke lone par principal amount or us par lagane vaale byaaj ko beshart bhugtan karnaa sweekaar karata he
 When lou is issued, it includes the issuing bank, the accepting bank, the importer and the company benefiting from it abroad
 pienbi ke maamlemen farji lou hasil kiye gaye or inhen ke aadhaar par exis or elahabaad jaise bainkon kii videshi shakhaon se lone liye gaye the

 An Indian astronomer has claimed that a recent discovery by the US Space Research Agency NASA confirms his theory of black holes
 bhartiya vaigyanik kaa kahana he ki tathakthith taur par blike hole kahe jane vaale khagol pind vastav main blike hole nahin, balki hamaare surya kii tarah dahakate aag ke gole hote hai or haal hi main nasa ke vaigyanikon ne ek blike hole se eks kirnon kii vishaal lapten dekhi, jisase unke siddhant kii pushti hoti he
 According to astronomers, even the most massive astrophysic bodies are contained in a very dense black hole (krishna Vivara), because the gravity of a black hole is so high that even light cannot reach beyond its limits
 nasa dwaara pichley maheene yah khulaasa karnaa ek aashcharya kii tarah dekha gaya ki nasa ke do antariksh doorabeenon ne ek atyant vishaal blike hole se eks kirnon kii vishaal lapten nikalati dekhi
 These huge flames of x rays emanating from the black hole were different in the sense that they were emitted by a massive explosion in the black hole's corona
 aise main yah sawaal uthanaa lajimi he ki yadi blike hole se kuch bhi baahar nahin aa saktaa to corona kaise baahar aayaa? a few days ago, the president of theoretical astronomy at the Bhabha Atomic Research Center in Mumbai, and now Assistant Professor at Homi Bhabha National Institute, Abhaas Mitra says that this new discovery from NASA only confirms his theory that in the universe No 'real' black hole exists and what we call as black holes, those astro bodies are actually magnetic plas Ma's terribly hot shells
 tippaniyan Mitra elaborated that when a superstar hits a black hole, the radiation in that extremely hot star creates an outward force against gravity, resulting in a very slow contraction
 is tarah oinstin ke siddhant main jise blike hole kaha gaya, use ham vishalkay taare ke sankuchit hone se nirmit behad garm aag kaa gola yaa 'magnetospherick itarnali colapsing objects' (emisio) kah sakate hai
 He said that fresh evidence in support of this new theory has been published in leading research journals since 2000
 unhone kaha, "chumbakeey gole kaa hamaare paas sabase acha udhaaharan hamaare soramandal kaa hi surya tara he, jiske chaaron ore behad patali plasma kii part he jise corona kehete hai

 " khagolavidon ke anusaar, atyant vishaal khagol pind bhi behad saghan pind blike hole (krishna vivar) main samaa jate hai, kyonki blike hole kaa gurutvkarshan itnaa adhik hota he ki prakaash tak uski seemaa se baahar nahin nikal paata
